                                    1831             +*/* 1) A REQUEST BLOCK POINTER. THIS IS A FULLWORD CONTAINING THE    */
                                    1832             +*/*    ADDRESS OF THE DYNAMIC ALLOCATION REQUEST BLOCK. THE HIGH-    */
                                    1833             +*/*    ORDER BIT MUST BE ON. THIS WORD MUST BE LOCATED BY REG. ONE.  */
                                    1834             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    1835             +*/* 2) A REQUEST BLOCK. THIS BLOCK IS LOCATED BY THE REQUEST BLOCK   */
                                    1836             +*/*    POINTER AND CONTAINS:                                         */
                                    1837             +*/*    . A ONE BYTE FIELD CONTAINING THE LENGTH OF THIS REQUEST      */
                                    1838             +*/*      BLOCK. THE LENGTH IS IN BINARY AND HAS A VALUE OF 20.       */
                                    1839             +*/*    . A ONE BYTE FIELD CONTAINING A VERB CODE CORRESPONDING TO A  */
                                    1840             +*/*      DYNAMIC ALLOCATION FUNCTION. MNEMONIC NAMES FOR THE VERB    */
                                    1841             +*/*      CODES ARE CONTAINED IN THIS MACRO.                          */
                                    1842             +*/*    . TWO BYTES OF FLAGS WHICH MUST MAP DIRECTLY TO ALCFNCMAP     */
                                    1843             +*/*      (COMMON ALLOCATION FUNCTION MAP) IN IEFZB4D7.               */
                                    1844             +*/*    . TWO BYTES IN WHICH DYNAMIC ALLOCATION WILL RETURN AN ERROR  */
                                    1845             +*/*      REASON CODE.                                                */
                                    1846             +*/*    . TWO BYTES IN WHICH DYNAMIC ALLOCATION WILL RETURN AN        */

0                                   2202             +*/*      of the Dynamic Allocation functions.  The keys are used     */
                                    2203             +*/*      in the text unit input to Dynamic Allocation.  A key        */
                                    2204             +*/*      identifies the information being passed in a particular     */
                                    2205             +*/*      text unit.  A key is two bytes in length.  The names        */
                                    2206             +*/*      for the keys consist of:                                    */
                                    2207             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2208             +*/*      - The character 'D' representing Dynamic Allocation.        */
                                    2209             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2210             +*/*      - Characters representing the Dynamic Allocation            */
                                    2211             +*/*        function.  The functions are represented by these         */
                                    2212             +*/*        characters:                                               */
                                    2213             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2214             +*/*        - 'AL' for allocation,                                    */
                                    2215             +*/*        - 'UN' for unallocation,                                  */
                                    2216             +*/*        - 'CC' for concatenation,                                 */
                                    2217             +*/*        - 'DC' for deconcatenation,                               */
                                    2218             +*/*        - 'RI' for remove in-use,                                 */
                                    2219             +*/*        - 'DN' for ddname allocation,                             */
                                    2220             +*/*        - 'IN' for information retrieval input, and               */
                                    2221             +*/*        - 'INR' for information retrieval output.                 */
                                    2222             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2223             +*/*      - Descriptive characters (up to five).                      */
                                    2224             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2225             +*/*01* INVOCATION ****************************************************/
                                    2226             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2227             +*/*01* METHOD OF ACCESS =                                        @L6C*/

0                                   2654             +*/* SMCATIOT field of the SMCA data area (master scheduler TIOT)     */
                                    2655             +*/*01* SERIALIZATION: ENQ on SYSZTIOT                                */
                                    2656             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2657             +*/*01* FUNCTION: Provides the I/O support routines with pointers     */
                                    2658             +*/*    to JFCBs and to allocated devices.                            */
                                    2659             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2660             +*/*02* -  Each DD statement, whether it is a member of a         @P2A*/
                                    2661             +*/*       concatenation or not, has its own TIOT DD Entry. There @P2A*/
                                    2662             +*/*       will be one DD statement for each GDG data set for a   @P2A*/
                                    2663             +*/*       GDGALL request.                                        @P2A*/
                                    2664             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2665             +*/*02* -  Within each DD Entry there will be one Device Entry    @P2A*/
                                    2666             +*/*       for each device allocated to that DD statement.        @P2A*/
                                    2667             +*/*       Single device does not always mean "not a multi-volume"@P2A*/
                                    2668             +*/*       data set.  For permres devices (e.g., D/T3390), device @P2A*/
                                    2669             +*/*       and volume are synonymous.  However, for tape requests @P2A*/
                                    2670             +*/*       device and volume are NOT synonymous since a tape      @P2A*/
                                    2671             +*/*       volume can be mounted on any one of many tape devices. @P2A*/
                                    2672             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2673             +*/*01* METHOD OF ACCESS:                                             */
                                    2674             +*/*      A DSECT card should precede the macro call. USING on        */
                                    2675             +*/*      TIOT1 gives addressability for all symbols.                 */
                                    2676             +*/*01* METHOD OF PL/S ACCESS:                                        */
                                    2677             +*/*      PL/S - DCL TIOTPTR PTR                                      */
                                    2678             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2679             +*/*  DEPENDENCY - ANY CHANGES TO THE TIOENTRY STRUCTURE OF THIS  @L0A*/
                                    2680             +*/*               MAPPING SHOULD BE REFLECTED IN THE IPCS        @L0A*/
                                    2681             +*/*               MODEL IEFMTIOE.                                @L0A*/
                                    2682             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2683             +*/*  CHANGE ACTIVITY - L0                                            */
                                    2684             +*/*   $L0= DDPERF   HBB4420 900406 PDDS: DDLPERFIPCS DD LIMIT        */
                                    2685             +*/*                                                  PERFORMANCE @L0A*/
                                    2686             +*/*   $P1= PSD0454  JBB6602 950921 PDXB: Fix TIOEJFCB comment,   @P1A*/
                                    2687             +*/*                                      Add TIOCSTEP subfields. @P1A*/
                                    2688             +*/*   $P2= PSD0771  JBB6602 960208 PDNN: Updates to the prolog   @P2A*/
                                    2689             +*/*                                                                  */
